   Svayambhu Purāṇa	SvayamBu PurANa
   prathama adhyāya	praTamaH aDyAya
   svayambhūdharmadhātusamutpatti nidānakathā	svayamBU-Darma-DAtu-samutpatti nidAna-kaTA
   om namaḥ śrī dharmadhātuvāgīśvarāya sarva buddhadharmabodhisattvebhyaḥ /	om namaH SrI DarmaDAtu-vAgISvarAya sarva budDa-Darma-boDisattveByaH /
   śrīmatā yena saddharmastrailoke saṃprakāśitaḥ /	SrImatA yena sadDarmaH-trEloke saMprakASitaH /
   śrīghanaṃ taṃ mahābuddhaṃ vandeka'haṃ śaraṇāśritaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.1 //	SrIGanam tam mahAbudDam vandeka-aham SaraNa-ASritaH // SvayamBuj-_1.1 //
   natvā trijagadīśānaṃ dharmadhātujinālayaṃ /	natvA trijagat-ISAnam DarmaDAtu-jina-Alayam /
   tatsvayambhūsamuddeśaṃ vakṣāmi śṛṇutādarāt // SvayambhuP_1.2 //	tad-svayamBU-samuddeSam vakzAmi SRNuta-AdarAt // SvayamBuj-_1.2 //
   śraddhayā yaḥ śṛṇotīmāṃ svayambhūtpattisatkathāṃ /	SradDayA yaH SRNoti-imAm svayamBUt-patti-sat-kaTAm /
   pariśuddhatrikāyāḥ sa bodhisattvo bhaved dhruvaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.3 //	pariSudDa-trikAyAH sa boDisattvaH Bavet Druvam // SvayamBuj-_1.3 //
   tadyathā bhūtpurābhijñaḥ jayaśrī sugatātmajaḥ /	tat-yaTA BUt-pura-aBijQaH jaya-SrI sugata-AtmajaH /
   bodhimaṇḍavihāre sa bijahāra sasāṃdhikaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.4 //	boDimaNxa-vihAre sa bijahAra sa-sAMDikaH // SvayamBuj-_1.4 //
   tatra jineśvaro nāma bodhisattva mahāmatiḥ /	tatra jineSvaraH nAma boDisattva mahAmatiH /
   śraddhayā śaraṇaṃ gatvā jayaśrīyaṃ upāśrayet // SvayambhuP_1.5 //	SradDayA SaraNam gatvA jaya-SrIyam upASrayet // SvayamBuj-_1.5 //
   tadā dhīmānjayaśrīḥ sa sarvasattva hitārthavit /	tadA DImAn-jaya-SrIH sa sarva-sattva hita-arTa-vid /
   saddharmasamupādeṣṭuṃ sabhāsane samāśrayet // SvayambhuP_1.6 //	sadDarma-samupAdezwum saBAsane samASrayet // SvayamBuj-_1.6 //
   tatra sarve mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ /	tatra sarve mahAsattvAH boDisattvAH jina-AtmajAH /
   arhanto bhikṣavaścāpi brahmacāriṇaḥ śrāvakāḥ // SvayambhuP_1.7 //	arhantaH BikzavaH-ca-api brahmacAriNaH SrAvakAH // SvayamBuj-_1.7 //
   bhikṣuṇyo brahmacāriṇyo bratinaścāpyupāsakāḥ /	BikzuNyaH brahmacAriNyaH bratinaH-ca-api-upAsakAH /
   upāsikāstathānye 'pi gṛhasthaśca mahājanāḥ // SvayambhuP_1.8 //	upAsikAH-taTA-anye api gRhasTaH-ca mahAjanAH // SvayamBuj-_1.8 //
   brāhmaṇāstirthīkāścāpi yatayaśca tapasvinaḥ /	brAhmaNAH-tirTIkAH-ca-api yatayaH-ca tapasvinaH /
   rājāno mantriṇomātyāḥ sainyādhipatiśca paurikāḥ // SvayambhuP_1.9 //	rAjAnaH mantriNaH-mAtyAH sEnya-aDipatiH-ca pOrikAH // SvayamBuj-_1.9 //
   grāmyā janapadāścāpi tathānyavāsino janāḥ /	grAmyAH janapadAH-ca-api taTA-anya-vAsinaH janAH /
   tatsaddharmāmṛtaṃ pātuṃ śraddhayā samupāgatāḥ // SvayambhuP_1.10 //	tad-sadDarma-amRtam pAtum SradDayA samupAgatAH // SvayamBuj-_1.10 //
   tatra sabhāsanāsīnaṃ tamarhataṃ jayaśrīyaṃ /	tatra saBAsana-AsInam tam-arhatam jaya-SrIyam /
   abhyarcya sādaraṃ natvā tatsabhāyāṃ yathākramaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.11 //	aByarcya sa-Adaram natvA tad-saBAyAm yaTAkramam // SvayamBuj-_1.11 //
   kṛtāṃjalipuṭāḥ sarve parivṛtya samantataḥ /	kRta-aMjali-puwAH sarve parivRtya samantataH /
   puraskṛtya samudvikṣya samāśrayan samāhitāḥ // SvayambhuP_1.12 //	puraskRtya samudvikzya samASrayan samAhitAH // SvayamBuj-_1.12 //
   tān sarvān samupāsīnān saddharma śravaṇotsukān /	tAn sarvAn samupAsInAn sadDarma SravaNa-utsukAn /
   dṛṣṭvā jinaśrī bodhisattvaḥ samutthitaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.13 //	dRzwvA jina-SrI boDisattvaH samutTitaH // SvayamBuj-_1.13 //
   udvahannuttarāsaṃgaṃ sāṃjali samupāśritaḥ /	udvahan=-uttarAsaMgam sAMjali samupASritaH /
   jānubhyāṃ bhūtale dhṛtvā sampaśyannevamavravīt // SvayambhuP_1.14 //	jAnuByAm BU-tale DRtvA sampaSyan=-evam-avravIt // SvayamBuj-_1.14 //
   bhadantoharṣamicchāmi carituṃ bodhisaṃvaraṃ /	BadantaH-harzam-icCAmi caritum boDi-saMvaram /
   tadādau kiṃ vrataṃ dhṛtvā saṃcareya samāhitaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.15 //	tad-AdO kim vratam DRtvA saMcareya samAhitaH // SvayamBuj-_1.15 //
   tad bhavān samupādisya sarvānasmān prabodhayan /	tat BavAn samupAdisya sarvAn-asmAn praboDayan /
   bodhimārge samāyujya cārayituṃ śubherhati // SvayambhuP_1.16 //	boDi-mArge samAyujya cArayitum SuBeH-hati // SvayamBuj-_1.16 //
   iti saṃprārthitaṃ tena śrutvā ca sugatātmajaḥ /	iti saMprArTitam tena SrutvA ca sugata-AtmajaH /
   jayaśrīstaṃ mahāsattvaṃ sabhāmantraivamādiśat // SvayambhuP_1.17 //	jaya-SrIH-tam mahAsattvam saBA-mantra-evam-AdiSat // SvayamBuj-_1.17 //
   śṛṇu vatsāsti te vāṃchā sambodhisaṃvare yadi /	SRNu vatsa-asti te vA-aMCA samboDi-saMvare yadi /
   yathākramaṃ pravakṣāmi saṃbodhivratasādhanaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.18 //	yaTAkramam pravakzAmi saMboDi-vrata-sADanam // SvayamBuj-_1.18 //
   yo vāṃchā tatra saṃsāre carituṃ bodhisaṃvaraṃ /	yaH vA-aMCA tatra saMsAre caritum boDi-saMvaram /
   sa ādau śaraṇaṃ gatvā sadguruṃ samupāśrayeta // SvayambhuP_1.19 //	saH AdO SaraNam gatvA sat-gurum samupASrayeta // SvayamBuj-_1.19 //
   tadupadeśamāsādya yathāvidyi samāhitaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.20 //	tat-upadeSam-AsAdya yaTA-vidyi samAhitaH // SvayamBuj-_1.20 //
   tīrthe snātvā viśuddhātmā triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatāḥ /	tIrTe snAtvA viSudDa-AtmA tri-ratna-SaraNam gatAH /
   yathāvidhi samabhyarcya saṃbodhi nihitāśayaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.21 //	yaTAviDi samaByarcya saMboDi nihita-ASayaH // SvayamBuj-_1.21 //
   upoṣadhaṃvratamādhāya samācarejjagaddhite /	upozaDaMvratam-ADAya samAcaret-jagat-hite /
   evaṃ yaścarate nityaṃ saṃbodhimānasaḥ sudhīḥ // SvayambhuP_1.22 //	evam yaH-carate nityam saMboDi-mAnasaH suDIH // SvayamBuj-_1.22 //
   pariśuddha trikāyaḥ sa bodhisattve bhaved /	pariSudDa tri-kAyaH sa boDisattve Bavet /
   bodhisattvo mahāsattvaḥ sarvvasattva hitārthabhṛt // SvayambhuP_1.23 //	boDisattvaH mahAsattvaH sarvu-asattva hita-arTa-BRt // SvayamBuj-_1.23 //
   kramātsaṃbodhi saṃbhāraṃ saṃpūrayet samāhitaḥ /	kramAt-saMboDi saMBAram saMpUrayet samAhitaH /
   etatpuṇyābhiyuktātmācaturbrahma vihāradhṛk // SvayambhuP_1.24 //	etat-puNya-aBiyukta-AtmA-catur-brahma vihAra-DRk // SvayamBuj-_1.24 //
   niḥkleśo nirjjayanmārona saṃbodhiḥ samavāpnuyāt // SvayambhuP_1.25 //	niHkleSaH nirjjayat-mArona saMboDiH samavApnuyAt // SvayamBuj-_1.25 //
   evaṃ sarvatra lokeṣu saddharma saṃprakāśayan /	evam sarvatra lokezu sadDarma saMprakASayan /
   samāpya saugataṃkārya sunirvṛtimavāpnuyāt // SvayambhuP_1.26 //	samApya sOgataMkArya su-nirvRtim-avApnuyAt // SvayamBuj-_1.26 //
   tato 'rhaṃ sugato bhūtvā sarvvānsattvānpravodhayan /	tatas arham sugataH BUtvA sarvvAn-sattvAn-pravoDayan /
   bodhimārge pratiṣṭhāpya saṃvṛttau saṃpracārayet // SvayambhuP_1.27 //	boDi-mArge pratizWApya saMvRttO saMpracArayet // SvayamBuj-_1.27 //
   evaṃ sarve 'pi saṃbuddhāḥ yetītā apyanāgatāḥ /	evam sarve api saMbudDAH yeti-itAH api-anAgatAH /
   varttamānāśca te hayetad vratapuṇya vipākataḥ // SvayambhuP_1.28 //	varttamAnAH-ca te hayetat vratapuNya vipAkataH // SvayamBuj-_1.28 //
   bodhiprāpya jinā āsanbhaviṣyanti bhavantyapi /	boDi-prApya jinAH Asan-Bavizyanti Bavanti-api /
   evaṃ sarve mahāsattvā bodhisattvā jinātmajāḥ // SvayambhuP_1.29 //	evam sarve mahAsattvAH boDisattvAH jina-AtmajAH // SvayamBuj-_1.29 //
   arhanto 'pi thā sarve pariśuddhatrimaṇḍalāḥ /	arhantaH api TA sarve pariSudDa-tri-maNxalAH /
   bodhiṃ prāpya sunirvāṇaṃ yātā yāsyanti yāntyataḥ // SvayambhuP_1.30 //	boDim prApya su-nirvANam yAtAH yAsyanti yAnti-atas // SvayamBuj-_1.30 //
   evaṃ yūyaṃ parijñāya yadecchatha sunivṛtiṃ /	evam yUyam parijQAya yadA-icCaTa su-nivRtim /
   triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saṃcaradhvamidaṃ vrataṃ // SvayambhuP_1.31 //	tri-ratna-SaraNam gatvA saMcaraDvam-idam vratam // SvayamBuj-_1.31 //
   iti tena samādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa sugatātmajaḥ /	iti tena samAdizwam SrutvA sa sugata-AtmajaH /
   jineśvaraṃ tamarhantaṃ sampaśyannevamavravīt // SvayambhuP_1.32 //	jineSvaram tam-arhantam sampaSyan=-evam-avravIt // SvayamBuj-_1.32 //
   bhadanta śrotumichāmi tad vratasthānamuttamaṃ /	Badanta Srotum-iCAmi tat vrata-sTAnam-uttamam /
   etad vrataṃ caretkutra taddeśaṃ samupādiśat // SvayambhuP_1.33 //	etat vratam caret-kutra tad-deSam samupAdiSat // SvayamBuj-_1.33 //
   iti saṃprārthite tena jayaśrīḥ sa mahāmatiḥ /	iti saMprArTite tena jaya-SrIH sa mahAmatiH /
   jineśvaraṃ mahāsattvaṃ taṃ paśyannevamādiśat // SvayambhuP_1.34 //	jineSvaram mahAsattvam tam paSyan=-evam-AdiSat // SvayamBuj-_1.34 //
   śṛṇu vatsa samādhāyaṃ vratasthānasamuttamaṃ /	SRNu vatsa samADAyam vrata-sTAna-samuttamam /
   munīśvarairyathākhyātaṃ tathā vakṣāmi te 'dhunā // SvayambhuP_1.35 //	muni-ISvarEH-yaTA-AKyAtam taTA vakzAmi te aDunA // SvayamBuj-_1.35 //
   puṇyakṣetreṣu tīrtheṣu vihāre sugatāśrame //	puNya-kzetrezu tIrTezu vihAre sugata-ASrame //
   buddhānāṃ nivṛtānāṃca caityeṣu pratimāsu ca // SvayambhuP_1.36 //	budDAnAm nivRtAnAMca cEtyezu pratimAsu ca // SvayamBuj-_1.36 //
   buddhakṣetreṣu sarvatra vratasthānaṃ samuttamaṃ /	budDa-kzetrezu sarvatra vrata-sTAnam samuttamam /
   eteṣvami samākhyātaṃ svayambhūcaityaṃ uttamaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.37 //	etezu-ami samAKyAtam svayamBU-cEtyam uttamam // SvayamBuj-_1.37 //
   evaṃ vijñāya yo dhīmānvrataṃ caritumicchati /	evam vijQAya yaH DImAn-vratam caritum-icCati /
   sa svayambhū jinakṣetraṃ āśritya caratāṃ vrataṃ // SvayambhuP_1.38 //	sa svayamBU jina-kzetram ASritya caratAm vratam // SvayamBuj-_1.38 //
   svayambhūkṣetramāśritya yaścarati vrataṃ mudā /	svayamBU-kzetram-ASritya yaH-carati vratam mudA /
   sa labhet tanmahat puṇyamakṣayaṃ bodhisādhanaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.39 //	sa laBet tat-mahat puNyam-akzayam boDi-sADanam // SvayamBuj-_1.39 //
   etat puṇyaṃ viśuddhātmā bhadraśrī sadguṇāśrayaḥ /	etat puNyam viSudDa-AtmA BadraSrI sat-guNa-ASrayaH /
   bodhisattvo mahābhijñā bhavajjinātmajo dhruvaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.40 //	boDisattvaH mahA-aBijQA Bavat-jina-AtmajaH Druvam // SvayamBuj-_1.40 //
   durgatiṃ na brajet kvāpi saṃsāre sa kadācana /	durgatim na brajet kvApi saMsAre sa kadAcana /
   sadā sadgatisaṃjāto bodhicaryāvrataṃ caret // SvayambhuP_1.41 //	sadA sat-gati-saMjAtaH boDi-caryA-vratam caret // SvayamBuj-_1.41 //
   evaṃ sa saṃsaralloke kṛtvā sarvatra bhadratā /	evam sa saMsarat-loke kRtvA sarvatra BadratA /
   saṃbodhi praṇidhiṃ dhṛtvā saṃcare tadjagaddhite // SvayambhuP_1.42 //	saMboDi praNiDim DRtvA saMcare tad-jagat-hite // SvayamBuj-_1.42 //
   evaṃ ca bodhi saṃbhāraṃ pūrayitvā yathākramaṃ /	evam ca boDi saMBAram pUrayitvA yaTAkramam /
   trividhāṃ bodhimāsādyaḥ nirvṛtipadamāpnuyāt // SvayambhuP_1.43 //	triviDAm boDim-AsAdyaH nirvRti-padam-ApnuyAt // SvayamBuj-_1.43 //
   evaṃ yūyaṃ parijñātvāḥ svayambhūsthāna āśritā /	evam yUyam parijQAtvAH svayamBU-sTAnaH ASritAH /
   triratnaśaraṇaṃ gatvā saṃcaratha vratottamaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.44 //	tri-ratna-SaraNam gatvA saMcaraTa vrata-uttamam // SvayamBuj-_1.44 //
   etattenārhatādiṣṭaṃ śrutvā sa sugatātmajaḥ /	etat-tena-arhata-Adizwam SrutvA sa sugata-AtmajaH /
   jayaśriyaṃ tamarhantaṃ sampaśyannevamabravīt // SvayambhuP_1.45 //	jaya-Sriyam tam-arhantam sampaSyan=-evam-abravIt // SvayamBuj-_1.45 //
   bhadanta bhavatā diṣṭaṃ śrutvā me rocate manaḥ /	Badanta BavatA dizwam SrutvA me rocate manaH /
   svayambhūcaityamārādhya carituṃ vratamābhavaṃ // SvayambhuP_1.46 //	svayamBU-cEtyam-ArADya caritum vratam-ABavam // SvayamBuj-_1.46 //
   svayambhū caityarājaḥ śrīdharmadhātu jinālayaḥ /	svayamBU cEtya-rAjaH SrI-DarmaDAtu jina-AlayaH /
   kutrāstyatra mahīloke tat samādeṣṭumarhati // SvayambhuP_1.47 //	kutra-asti-atra mahI-loke tat samAdezwum-arhati // SvayamBuj-_1.47 //
   iti saprārthitaṃ tena śrutvāṃ so 'rhan yatiḥ sudhīḥ /	iti sa-prArTitam tena SrutvAm saH arhan yatiH suDIH /
   jayaśrī staṃ mahāsattva samālokyaivamādiśata // SvayambhuP_1.48 //	jaya-SrI stam mahA-sattva samAlokya-evam-AdiSata // SvayamBuj-_1.48 //
   vidyate 'tra mahīloke uttarasyāṃ himālaye /	vidyate atra mahI-loke uttarasyAm himAlaye /
   nepāla iti vikhyāteḥ gopucchākhyernagottamaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.49 //	nepAlaH iti viKyAteH go-pucCa-AKyeH-naga-uttamaH // SvayamBuj-_1.49 //
   tadgirernāma cāturdhya caturyugeṣu vartate /	tat-gireH-nAma cAturDya caturyugezu vartate /
   tadyathābhūdyuge satye padmagiririti smṛtaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.50 //	tat-yaTA-aBUt-yuge satye padmagiriH-iti smRtaH // SvayamBuj-_1.50 //
   tretāyāṃ vajrakūṭākhyo gośṛṃgo dvāpare smṛtaḥ /	tretAyAm vajrakUwa-AKyaH go-SRMgaH dvApare smRtaH /
   idānīṃ tu kalau 'sau gopuccha iti viśrutaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.51 //	idAnIm tu kalO asO gopucCaH iti viSrutaH // SvayamBuj-_1.51 //
   so 'piśailo idānītu lokai nepāla deśakaiḥ /	saH api-SElaH idAnItu lokEH nepAla deSakEH /
   sāmheguriti vikhyāta stathāsaṃprasthito bhuvi // SvayambhuP_1.52 //	sAmheguH-iti viKyAta staTA-saMprasTitaH Buvi // SvayamBuj-_1.52 //
   sa sarvadhāturalādi sarvadravyamayoktamaḥ /	sa sarva-DAtuH-ala-Adi sarva-dravyam-aya-uktamaH /
   aśvattha pramukhairsavairpādapaiḥ saṃpraśobhitaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.53 //	aSvatTa pramuKEH-savEH-pAdapEH saMpraSoBitaH // SvayamBuj-_1.53 //
   sarvatra kusumairkāntaḥ saṃrvoṣadhiphaladrumaiḥ /	sarvatra kusumEH-kAntar saMrvozaDi-Pala-drumEH /
   sarvapakṣivirāvaiścaḥ bhramadbhramaranisvanaiḥ // SvayambhuP_1.54 //	sarva-pakzi-virAvEH-caH Bramat-Bramara-nisvanEH // SvayamBuj-_1.54 //
   jantubhiḥ sakalaḥ sneha nivaddhamaitramānasaiḥ /	jantuBiH sakalaH sneha nivadDa-mEtra-mAnasEH /
   tapasvivaddhayā bhadracāribhiḥ saniṣevitaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.55 //	tapasvi-vat-DayA BadracAriBiH sa-nizevitaH // SvayamBuj-_1.55 //
   aṣṭāṃga guṇasaṃpanna saṃśuddhāmṛtanirjharaiḥ /	azwAMga guNa-saMpad-na saMSudDa-amRta-nirJarEH /
   śobhitaḥ puṣpagaṃdhādhi saṃvāsitaiḥ samīraṇaiḥ // SvayambhuP_1.56 //	SoBitaH puzpa-gaMDa-aDi saMvAsitEH samIraNEH // SvayamBuj-_1.56 //
   saṃsevitaḥ sadā divya mahotsāhairvivājitaḥ /	saMsevitaH sadA divya mahA-utsAhEH-vivAjitaH /
   sarvalokādhipairnityaṃ saṃsevitaḥ samādaraiḥ // SvayambhuP_1.57 //	sarva-loka-aDipEH-nityam saMsevitaH samAdarEH // SvayamBuj-_1.57 //
   tatra ratnamaya padmaḥ karṇṇikāyāṃ samāśritaḥ /	tatra ratna-maya padmaH karNNikAyAm samASritaH /
   divya sphaṭikaratnābhajyotirūpo nirañjanaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.58 //	divya sPawika-ratna-ABajyoti-rUpaH niraQjanaH // SvayamBuj-_1.58 //
   ekahastaḥ pramānoccaścaityarūpo jināśrayaḥ /	eka-hastaH pramAna-uccaH-cEtya-rUpaH jina-ASrayaH /
   svayambhūḥ sarvalokānāṃ bhadrārtha samavasthitaḥ // SvayambhuP_1.59 //	svayamBUH sarva-lokAnAm Badra-arTa samavasTitaH // SvayamBuj-_1.59 //
   brahma śakrādibhirdevaiḥ sarvaillokādhipairapi /	brahma Sakra-AdiBiH-devEH sarvElloka-aDipEH-api /
   sarvairdaityādhipaiścāpi nāgendraiḥ garuḍairapi // SvayambhuP_1.60 //	sarvEH-dEtya-aDipEH-ca-api nAga-indrEH garuxEH-api // SvayamBuj-_1.60 //
   siddhai vidyādharaiḥ sādhyairūryakṣagandharvakinnaraiḥ /	sidDEH vidyADarEH sADyEH-Uryakza-ganDarva-kinnarEH /
